<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a> (13624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-рыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взорвать.html>взорва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow up, to detonate, to blast
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzryvátʹ</b> zarjád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set off a charge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enrage, to exasperate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also used impersonally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Их</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оскорбление.html>оскорбле́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ix <b>vzryválo</b> za oskorblénije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They were boiling with rage at the insult.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывать.html>взрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрываться.html>взрыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взорваться.html>взорва́ться</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывно́й</a> (11752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрыв.html>взрыв</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzryv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzryvnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> explosive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzryvnája</b> volná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">air blast; shock wave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывны́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzryvnýje</b> rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blasting; blasting operations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> explosive, violent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:характер.html>хара́ктер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzryvnój</b> xarákter</i> ― <span class="e-translation">explosive temper</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plosive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взрывной.html>взрывны́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:согласный.html>согла́сные</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzryvnýje</b> soglásnyje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(ex)plosive/stop consonants</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a> (10717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with reduction of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*взз-</span> to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вз-</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвать.html>воззва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to appeal <i>(to someone for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyvátʹ</b> o pómošči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to call for help</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взывать.html>взыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:справедливость.html>справедли́вости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyvátʹ</b> o spravedlívosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to demand justice</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взыграть.html>взыгра́ть</a> (28087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыграть.html>взыгра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzygrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взы́грывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start frolicking, to jump for joy</li>
<li>to swell <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the sea, wind, a river, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to manifest strongly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a feeling</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to swell <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of pride</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to leap <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the heart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ние</a> (17063)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzyskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzyskánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>penalty, punishment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наложить.html>наложи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ние</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naložítʹ <b>vzyskánije</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">impose a penalty; inflict a punishment</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвергнуться.html>подве́ргнуться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́нию</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvérgnutʹsja <b>vzyskániju</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">incur a penalty</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>recovery, exaction
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:издержка.html>изде́ржек</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyskánije</b> izdéržek</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">cost recovery</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искать.html>иска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzyskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взы́скивать</b>)

<ol><li>to exact <i>(from, of)</i>, to recover <i>(from)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzyskátʹ</b> dolg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to recover a debt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make answer <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взыскать.html>взыщи́те</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne vzyščíte!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">please forgive me!; don't be hard on me!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>взыс<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***взять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> (138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъzęti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взимать.html>взима́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взыма́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>шту́рмом</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzjatʹ</b> štúrmom štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to take</b> something by storm</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vzjatʹ</b> k sebé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take in</span></div></dd>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 14b/c'.     <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рме</a> прош. вр. <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́днего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наравне.html>наравне́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмой</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взя́ло</a></i>» <a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>возмо́жна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взяло́</a></i>». <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a>, взымать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-взя-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>вз-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-я-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://i46.fastpic.ru/big/2013/0718/4d/59f2e0a394dd0dd5ab85ffdca1c3e84d.jpg">Кузнецова <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Ефремова</a></sup>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>взя́ться</a> (1176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>взя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vzjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:браться.html>бра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take something with hands, to take (mutually, together) (e.g. each other's hands)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>Возьмёмся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзья́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтоб.html>чтоб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поодиночке.html>поодино́чке</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vozʹmjómsja</b> zá ruki, druzʹjá, štob ne propástʹ poodinóčke.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let's <b>take</b> each other's hands, my friends, so that we don't perish one by one.</span></dd></dl></div> (<i>Bulat Okudzhava</i>, a song)</dd></dl></li>
<li>to set about; to undertake (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative case <i>a task</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льника</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>возьму́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S ponedélʹnika <b>vozʹmúsʹ</b> za anglíjskij jazýk.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">From Monday I'll <b>tackle</b> English.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appear, to emerge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:откуда.html>отку́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>возьму́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jésli ne xvatájet déneg sevódnja, otkúda oní <b>vozʹmútsja</b> závtra?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">If there's not enough money today, where will it <b>come from</b> tomorrow?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vzjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взя́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 14b/c".      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:браться.html>бра́ться</a>, взыматься.

***вибрировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вибрировать.html>вибри́ровать</a> (14813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вибрировать.html>вибри́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vibrírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завибрировать.html>завибри́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to vibrate, to oscillate</li>
<li>to quaver</li>
<li>to shimmy</li>
<li>to thrill</li>
<li>to flutter</li>
<li>to jar</li>
<li>to pulsate</li>
<li>to chatter</li></ol>

***вид.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a> (176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">видъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vidŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vidъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know; see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">veidas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">face</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">veids</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form, shape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">वेद</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knowledge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬬𐬀𐬉𐬛𐬀𐬵</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vaēdah-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">possession</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">videō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἶδος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eîdos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form, shape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">fíad</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">gŵydd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">presence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*weido-</i>), and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">witan</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wit</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vid</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>look, looks, appearance, air</li>
<li>sight, view
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́де</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri <b>víde</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the sight of</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>виду́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>vidú</b> u</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in sight; visible to</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́ду</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>vídu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by sight; judging from appearance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́дом</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:виданный.html>ви́дано</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto <b>vídom</b> ne vídano</i> ― <span class="e-translation">"never seen before"</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto xorošó na <b>vid</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">"that looks fine"</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>kind, sort, species</li>
<li>form
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письменный.html>пи́сьменном</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́де</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v písʹmennom <b>víde</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in written form</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прежний.html>пре́жнем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́де</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v préžnem <b>víde</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in previous form</span></div></dd>
